      <p>
       <b>
        Mercosur
       </b>
       (also known as
       <b>
        Mercosul
       </b>
       or
       <b>
        Ñemby Ñemuha
       </b>
       )
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">
        <a href="#cite_note-7">
         [7]
        </a>
       </sup>
       is a
       <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">
        South American
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Trade_bloc" title="Trade bloc">
        trade bloc
       </a>
       established by the
       <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Treaty of Asunción">
        Treaty of Asunción
       </a>
       in 1991 and
       <a href="/wiki/Protocol_of_Ouro_Preto" title="Protocol of Ouro Preto">
        Protocol of Ouro Preto
       </a>
       in 1994. Its full members are
       <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">
        Argentina
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">
        Brazil
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">
        Paraguay
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">
        Uruguay
       </a>
       .
       <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">
        Venezuela
       </a>
       is a full member but has been suspended since December 1, 2016. Associate countries are
       <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">
        Bolivia
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">
        Chile
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">
        Peru
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">
        Colombia
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">
        Ecuador
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">
        Suriname
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">
        <a href="#cite_note-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Observer_status" title="Observer status">
        Observer countries
       </a>
       are
       <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">
        New Zealand
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">
        Mexico
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">
        <a href="#cite_note-9">
         [9]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">
        <a href="#cite_note-10">
         [10]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2801" data-file-width="4985" height="169" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg/300px-Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg/450px-Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg/600px-Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sede_del_MERCOSUR.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Headquarters of MERCOSUR, Montevideo, Uruguay, aerial view..
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Mercosur's purpose is to promote
       <a href="/wiki/Free_trade" title="Free trade">
        free trade
       </a>
       and the fluid movement of goods, people, and currency. The official languages are Spanish, Portuguese, and
       <a href="/wiki/Guarani_language" title="Guarani language">
        Guarani
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">
        <a href="#cite_note-11">
         [11]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Since its foundation, Mercosur's functions have been updated, amended, and changed many times: it is now a full
       <a href="/wiki/Customs_union" title="Customs union">
        customs union
       </a>
       and a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trading_bloc" title="Trading bloc">
        trading bloc
       </a>
       . Mercosur and the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Andean_Community_of_Nations" title="Andean Community of Nations">
        Andean Community of Nations
       </a>
       are customs unions that are components of a continuing process of South American
       <a href="/wiki/Economic_integration" title="Economic integration">
        integration
       </a>
       connected to the
       <a href="/wiki/Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="Union of South American Nations">
        Union of South American Nations
       </a>
       (USAN).
      </p>
      <p>
      </p>

      <p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="History">
        History
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Founding">
        Founding
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Founding">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Mercosur was established in 1991 by the
       <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Treaty of Asunción">
        Treaty of Asunción
       </a>
       , which was later amended and updated by the 1994
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Ouro_Preto" title="Treaty of Ouro Preto">
        Treaty of Ouro Preto
       </a>
       . Mercosur originated in 1988, when presidents
       <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_Alfons%C3%ADn" title="Raúl Alfonsín">
        Raúl Alfonsín
       </a>
       of Argentina and
       <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Sarney" title="José Sarney">
        José Sarney
       </a>
       of Brazil signed the
       <i>
        Argentina-Brazil Integration and Economics Cooperation Program
       </i>
       or
       <b>
        PICE
       </b>
       (Portuguese: Programa de Integração e Cooperação Econômica Argentina-Brasil, Spanish: Programa de Integración y Cooperación Económica Argentina-Brasil).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">
        <a href="#cite_note-12">
         [12]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The protocol Number 20 of the program also proposed the
       <a href="/wiki/Gaucho_(currency)" title="Gaucho (currency)">
        Gaucho
       </a>
       as a currency for regional trade.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
        <a href="#cite_note-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The founding of the
       <a href="/wiki/Mercosur_Parliament" title="Mercosur Parliament">
        Mercosur Parliament
       </a>
       was agreed upon at the December 2004 presidential summit. Up to 2010 it was planned to have 18 representatives from each country, regardless of population.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">
        <a href="#cite_note-14">
         [14]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Memberships_and_suspensions">
        Memberships and suspensions
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Memberships and suspensions">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       After suspending Paraguay in 2012, the presidents of the Mercosur countries (Argentina, Brazil, Uruguay, and Venezuela) said in July 2013 that they would lift the suspension after the inauguration of Paraguay's newly elected President, Horacio Cartes, on 15 August 2013. However, Paraguay said it would not return to the Mercosur fold as long as Venezuela held its rotating presidency. Venezuela held Mercosur's rotating presidency until July 2014. Paraguay has objected to Venezuela's inclusion in the trading bloc, and says that a new member can only be included after a unanimous vote and argues that such a vote should not have been held while Paraguay was suspended.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-President_Cartes_sworn_in_15-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-President_Cartes_sworn_in-15">
         [15]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Foreign Minister
       <a href="/wiki/Eladio_Loizaga" title="Eladio Loizaga">
        Eladio Loizaga
       </a>
       said he would rather deal with Paraguay's neighbours individually at first. "We have pending issues with Argentina, with Uruguay; we have to recompose all that," he said. "Mercosur will be later because our priority are  [
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Sic" title="Sic">
         sic
        </a>
       </i>
       ] the bilateral relations," he added.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-President_Cartes_sworn_in_15-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-President_Cartes_sworn_in-15">
         [15]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 7 December 2012, Bolivian President
       <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">
        Evo Morales
       </a>
       signed a protocol aimed at accession to full membership of the block.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
        <a href="#cite_note-16">
         [16]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Such a proposal requires review and possible legislative approval.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">
        <a href="#cite_note-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On July 7 of 2015, the heads of Mercosur having decided to accept Bolivia's request to become a full member country, Bolivian president Evo Morales signed the Brasilia protocol. This acted Bolivia's full membership to the Mercosur.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
        <a href="#cite_note-18">
         [18]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In August 2016, the presidents of Brazil, Argentina, and Paraguay, while present in Rio de Janeiro for the Olympic Games, met to discuss suspending Venezuela from Mercosur. The three countries were in doubt about whether Venezuela was complying with the union's requirements for full membership, citing Human Rights violations among other issues.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">
        <a href="#cite_note-19">
         [19]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In fact, Venezuela was rejected from assuming the presidency of Mercosur by those three countries, prompting a dispute that continued in full throttle to the end of the year.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
        <a href="#cite_note-20">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 21 November 2016, Paraguayan Foreign Minister
       <a href="/wiki/Eladio_Loizaga" title="Eladio Loizaga">
        Eladio Loizaga
       </a>
       announced that Venezuela would be suspended in December 2016 after the nation was given a three-month period to reform its laws to abide to Mercosur requirements, with Mercosur noting that "rules governing trade, politics, democracy and human rights" needed to be overhauled in Venezuela.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">
        <a href="#cite_note-21">
         [21]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On 1 December 2016, Venezuela was suspended from Mercosur.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-APvenSUS_22-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-APvenSUS-22">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Member_states">
        Member states
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Member states">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_Mercosur" title="Member states of Mercosur">
        Member states of Mercosur
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="9760" data-file-width="7504" height="286" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg/220px-Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg/330px-Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg/440px-Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg.png 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Miembros_de_Mercosur.svg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Member states, 31 July 2012.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Mercosur is composed of 5
       <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">
        sovereign
       </a>
       member states: Argentina; Brazil; Paraguay; Uruguay and Venezuela (suspended since December, 2016); and a state in process of incorporation, Bolivia (since July 17, 2015)
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">
        <a href="#cite_note-23">
         [23]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint noexcerpt Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTRS" title="Wikipedia:NOTRS">
          <span title="This claim needs references to better sources. (December 2016)">
           better source needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Following the
       <a href="/wiki/Impeachment_of_Fernando_Lugo" title="Impeachment of Fernando Lugo">
        impeachment of President Fernando Lugo
       </a>
       by the Paraguayan Senate, this country was suspended from Mercosur, and the admittance of Venezuela as a full member became effective on 31 July 2012.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-reuters.com_6-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-reuters.com-6">
         [6]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Venezuela had four years to fully adapt to the trade bloc regulations
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">
        <a href="#cite_note-24">
         [24]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and failed to do so, with the nation being suspended from Mercosur on 1 December 2016.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-APvenSUS_22-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-APvenSUS-22">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Directly subordinated to the Common Market Group, the Work Subgroups draw up the minutes of the decisions to submit for the consideration of the Council, and study specific Mercosur concerns. The work subgroups are:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Commercial matters
       </li>
       <li>
        Customs matters
       </li>
       <li>
        Technical standards
       </li>
       <li>
        Tax and monetary policies relating to trade
       </li>
       <li>
        Land transport
       </li>
       <li>
        Sea transport
       </li>
       <li>
        Industrial and technology policies
       </li>
       <li>
        Agricultural policy
       </li>
       <li>
        Energy policy
       </li>
       <li>
        Coordination of macroeconomic policies
       </li>
       <li>
        Labor, employment and social security matters
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Work subgroups are held quarterly, alternating in every member state, in alphabetical order, or at the Common Market Group Administrative Office. Activities are carried out by the Work Subgroups in two stages: preparatory and conclusive. In the preparatory stage, members of the Work Subgroups may request the participation of representatives from the private sector of each member state. The decision-making stage is reserved exclusively for official representatives of the member states. The delegations of representatives from the private sector in the preparatory stage of the Work Subgroup activities will have a maximum of three representatives for each member state directly involved in any of the stages of the production, distribution or consumption process for the products that fall within the scope of the subgroup's activities.,
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Heads_of_state">
        Heads of state
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Heads of state">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="center" style="width:auto; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto;">

           <div style="margin:15px auto;">

             <img alt="" data-file-height="3045" data-file-width="2214" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg/87px-Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg/131px-Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg/174px-Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="87"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="gallerytext">
           <p>
            <span class="flagicon">
             <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">
              <img alt="Argentina" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
             </a>
            </span>
            <b>
             <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">
              Argentina
             </a>
            </b>
            <br/>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">
        Geography
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Geography">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1106" data-file-width="5122" height="65" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg/300px-Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg/450px-Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg/600px-Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Iguazu_D%C3%A9cembre_2007_-_Panorama_7.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Iguazu_Falls" title="Iguazu Falls">
          Iguazu Falls
         </a>
         on the border between Argentina and Brazil is an area with
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Subtropical_climate" title="Subtropical climate">
          subtropical climate
         </a>
         and are one of the
         <a href="/wiki/New7Wonders_of_Nature" title="New7Wonders of Nature">
          New Seven World Natural Wonders
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The territory of Mercosur consists of the combined territories of six of the 12 countries of
       <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">
        South America
       </a>
       and their population. Including the overseas territories of member states, Mercosur experiences most
       <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">
        types of climate
       </a>
       from
       <a href="/wiki/Polar_climate" title="Polar climate">
        Antarctic
       </a>
       to
       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_climate" title="Tropical climate">
        tropical
       </a>
       , rendering meteorological averages for Mercosur as a whole meaningless. The majority of the population lives in areas with a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Subtropical_climate" title="Subtropical climate">
        subtropical climate
       </a>
       (Uruguay, Southern Paraguay, Northeastern Argentina and Southern and Southeastern Brazil), or a tropical climate (Venezuela and Northeastern Brazil).
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">
        Demographics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Demographics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3120" data-file-width="6032" height="129" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg/250px-Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg/375px-Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg/500px-Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg 2x" width="250"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Buenos_Aires_Cityline_at_Night_-_Irargerich.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">
          Buenos Aires
         </a>
         is the second largest city in South America. It is one of the only three "alpha" cities in Latin America, along with São Paulo and Mexico City,
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gawc_25-0">
          <a href="#cite_note-gawc-25">
           [25]
          </a>
         </sup>
         and it's the most visited city in South America.
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">
          <a href="#cite_note-26">
           [26]
          </a>
         </sup>
         It has the highest per capita income in the Southern Cone
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">
          <a href="#cite_note-27">
           [27]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <table class="wikitable">
       <caption>
        (
        <small>
         Sources
        </small>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-UN_WPP_28-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-UN_WPP-28">
          [28]
         </a>
        </sup>
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">
         <a href="#cite_note-29">
          [29]
         </a>
        </sup>
        )
       </caption>

        </th>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <p>
       The region is highly urbanized, and the largest cities in Mercosur are the
       <a href="/wiki/Global_city" title="Global city">
        global cities
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">
        Buenos Aires
       </a>
       , Rio de Janeiro and
       <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">
        São Paulo
       </a>
       . The white population is the majority in Argentina and CLGT and represents around half the population in Brazil. Venezuela's racial structure comprises 49.9% mestizo, while the other half about 42.2% of the country's population is considered white, less of 10% of the country's population is considered black, indigenous, Asian and others.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">
        <a href="#cite_note-30">
         [30]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Mestizos form the majority population in Paraguay.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bar_1-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-bar-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       All Mercosur nations have significant Native American populations, especially in Paraguay (Guaraní is a national language in the country along with Spanish, and almost all Paraguayans have Guaraní genetic ancestry), Argentina (especially in the country's North-Western, Northern, and Southern provinces), Brazil (in the Northern Amazonian states of the nation, where Native American tribes have vast reservation lands), Venezuela (in the
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Guayana_region&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Guayana region (page does not exist)">
        Guayana region
       </a>
       ).
      </p>
      <p>
       Along with Paraguay (where it is one of two official languages), sectors of Argentina (Corrientes) speak Guaraní. However, the Mercosur does not provide all, or even most, services in Guaraní. The official website, almost all official summits are only held in Spanish and Portuguese.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise_trade">
        Merchandise trade
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Merchandise trade">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Intra-Mercosur merchandise trade (excluding Venezuela) grew from US$10 billion at the inception of the trade bloc in 1991,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ege_31-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-ege-31">
         [31]
        </a>
       </sup>
       to US$88 billion in 2010; Brazil and Argentina each accounted for 43% of this total.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dg_32-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-dg-32">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The trade balance within the bloc has historically been tilted toward Brazil,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ege_31-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-ege-31">
         [31]
        </a>
       </sup>
       which recorded an intra-Mercosur balance of over US$5 billion in 2010.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dg_32-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-dg-32">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
        <a href="#cite_note-33">
         [33]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Trade within Mercosur amounted to only 16% of the four countries' total merchandise trade in 2010, however; trade with the European Union (20%), China (14%), and the United States (11%) was of comparable importance.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dg_32-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-dg-32">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Exports from the bloc are highly diversified, and include a variety of agricultural, industrial, and energy goods. Merchandise trade with the rest of the world in 2010 resulted in a surplus for Mercosur of nearly US$7 billion;
       <a href="/wiki/Trade_in_services" title="Trade in services">
        trade in services
       </a>
       , however, was in deficit by over US$28 billion.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dg_32-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-dg-32">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The EU and China maintained a nearly balanced merchandise trade with Mercosur in 2010, while the United States reaped a surplus of over US$14 billion; Mercosur, in turn, earned significant surpluses (over US$4 billion each in 2010) in its trade with Chile and Venezuela.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-dg_32-4">
        <a href="#cite_note-dg-32">
         [32]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The latter became a full member in 2012.
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Structure">
        Structure
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Structure">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <div style="width:52px">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/>
          </a>
         </div>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          This section
          <b>
           does not
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">
            cite
           </a>
           any
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">
            sources
           </a>
          </b>

           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">

      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:275px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Parque_Hotel,_Montevideo_23.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1200" height="182" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Parque_Hotel%2C_Montevideo_23.jpg/273px-Parque_Hotel%2C_Montevideo_23.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Parque_Hotel%2C_Montevideo_23.jpg/410px-Parque_Hotel%2C_Montevideo_23.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Parque_Hotel%2C_Montevideo_23.jpg/546px-Parque_Hotel%2C_Montevideo_23.jpg 2x" width="273"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Parque_Hotel,_Montevideo_23.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Headquarters of Mercosur, in the city of
         <a href="/wiki/Montevideo" title="Montevideo">
          Montevideo
         </a>
         , Uruguay.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Treaty of Asunción">
        Asunción Treaty
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Protocol_of_Ouro_Preto" title="Protocol of Ouro Preto">
        Ouro Preto Protocol
       </a>
       established the basis for the institutional Mercosur structure, creating the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Common_Market" title="Common Market">
        Common Market
       </a>
       Council and the Common Market Group, both of which function at the outset of the transition phase. As provided for in this Treaty, before establishing the common market the member nations must call a special meeting to determine the definitive institutional structure for the public agencies managing Mercosur, as well as define the specific functions of each agency and the decision making process.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Common_Market_Council">
        Common Market Council
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Common Market Council">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The Council is the highest-level agency of Mercosur with the authority to conduct its policy, and responsibility for compliance with the objects and time frames set forth in the Asuncion Treaty. The Council is composed of the
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs">
        Ministers of Foreign Affairs
       </a>
       and the Economy (or the equivalent) of all five countries. Member states preside over the Council in rotating alphabetical order, for six-month periods. Meetings: Council members shall meet whenever necessary, but at least once a year. The presidents of the member nations shall partake of the annual Common Market Council meeting whenever possible. Decision Making: Council decisions shall be made by consensus, with representation of all member states.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Common_Market_Group">
        Common Market Group
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Common Market Group">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hugo,_Dilma,_Pepe,_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="639" data-file-width="960" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Hugo%2C_Dilma%2C_Pepe%2C_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg/220px-Hugo%2C_Dilma%2C_Pepe%2C_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Hugo%2C_Dilma%2C_Pepe%2C_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg/330px-Hugo%2C_Dilma%2C_Pepe%2C_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Hugo%2C_Dilma%2C_Pepe%2C_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg/440px-Hugo%2C_Dilma%2C_Pepe%2C_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hugo,_Dilma,_Pepe,_Cristina_en_Mercosur.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The then-presidents of Venezuela, Brazil, Uruguay and Argentina together in
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brasilia" title="Brasilia">
          Brasilia
         </a>
         in 2012.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Group is the executive body of Mercosur, and is coordinated by the Ministries of Foreign Affairs of the member states. Its basic duties are to cause compliance with the Asuncion Treaty and to take resolutions required for implementation of the decisions made by the Council. Furthermore, it can initiate practical measures for trade opening, coordination of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Macroeconomic" title="Macroeconomic">
        macroeconomic
       </a>
       policies, and negotiation of agreements with nonmember states and international agencies, participating when need be in resolution of controversies under Mercosur. It has the authority to organize, coordinate and supervise Work Subgroups and to call special meetings to deal with issues of interest. Composition: The Common Market Group shall be made up of four permanent members and four alternates from each member state, representing the following
       <a href="/wiki/Public" title="Public">
        public
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Government_agency" title="Government agency">
        agencies
       </a>
       : (i) the
       <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs">
        Ministry of Foreign Affairs
       </a>
       ; (ii) the
       <a href="/wiki/Finance_minister" title="Finance minister">
        Ministry of Economy
       </a>
       , or the equivalent (from industry, foreign affairs and/or economic coordination); and (iii) the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Central_Bank" title="Central Bank">
        Central Bank
       </a>
       . The members of the Common Market Group appointed by a given member state will constitute the National Section of the Common Market Group for that particular nation. Meetings: The Common Market Group will meet ordinarily at least once every quarter in the member states, in rotating alphabetical order. Special meetings may be freely called at any time, at any previously scheduled place. The meetings will be coordinated by the Head of the Delegation of the host member state. Decision Making: Common Market Group decisions shall be made by consensus, with the representation of all member states. The official Mercosur languages will be Portuguese and Spanish, and the official version of all work papers will be prepared in the language of the country hosting the meeting.
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:194px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mercosul-Bandeira.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="320" data-file-width="192" height="320" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/67/Mercosul-Bandeira.jpg" width="192"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mercosul-Bandeira.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Mercosur/Mercosul's flag in the city of
         <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">
          Brasília
         </a>
         , Brazil.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_and_socioeconomic">
        Administrative and socioeconomic
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Administrative and socioeconomic">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The Administrative Office will keep documents and issue the Mercosur official bulletin in both Portuguese and Spanish, and will also be charged with communicating the activities of the Common Market Group so as to allow for the maximum disclosure of decisions and the relevant documentation. The
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Socioeconomic" title="Socioeconomic">
        Socioeconomic
       </a>
       Advisory Forum is consultative by nature, and represents the various socioeconomic sectors of the member nations.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Work_subgroups">
        Work subgroups
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Work subgroups">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Directly subordinated to the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Common_Market" title="Common Market">
        Common Market
       </a>
       Group, the Work Subgroups draw up the minutes of the decisions to submit for the consideration of the Council, and conduct studies on specific Mercosur concerns. The work subgroups are the following: commercial matters; customs matters; technical standards; tax and monetary policies relating to trade; land transport; sea transport; industrial and technology policies; agricultural policy; energy policy; coordination of macroeconomic policies; and labor, employment and social security matters. meetings. The meetings of the Work subgroups will be held quarterly, alternating in every member state, in alphabetical order, or at the Common Market Group Administrative Office. Activities will be carried out by the Work Subgroups in two stages: preparatory and conclusive. In the preparatory stage, the members of the Work Subgroups may request the participation of representatives from the private sector of each member state. The decision-making stage is reserved exclusively for official representatives of the member states. The delegations of representatives from the private sector in the preparatory stage of the Work Subgroup activities will have a maximum of three representatives for each member state directly involved in any of the stages of the production, distribution or consumption process for the products that fall within the scope of the subgroup's activities.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Joint_Parliamentary_Committee">
        Joint Parliamentary Committee
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Joint Parliamentary Committee">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1190" data-file-width="1999" height="131" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg/220px-Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg/330px-Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg/440px-Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mercosur_39_cumbre_en_San_Juan.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Presidents at 39th Mercosur summit at
         <a href="/wiki/San_Juan_Province,_Argentina" title="San Juan Province, Argentina">
          San Juan
         </a>
         , Argentina.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/Committee" title="Committee">
        Committee
       </a>
       will have both an advisory and decision-making nature; with powers to submit proposals as well. It will be competent, inter alia, to: follow up on the
       <a href="/wiki/Regional_integration" title="Regional integration">
        integration
       </a>
       process and keep the respective
       <a href="/wiki/Congress" title="Congress">
        Congresses
       </a>
       informed; Take the necessary steps for the future instatement of a
       <a href="/wiki/Mercosur_Parliament" title="Mercosur Parliament">
        Mercosur Parliament
       </a>
       ; Organize subcommittees to examine matters relating to the integration process; Submit its recommendations to the Common Market Council and Group as to how the integration process should be conducted and Southern Common Market formed; Make the adjustments necessary to harmonize the laws of the different member states and submit them to the respective Congresses; Establish relationships with private entities in each of the member states, as well as international agencies and bureaus so as to obtain information and specialized assistance with matters of interest: Establish relationships targeting cooperation with Congresses of the nonmember nations and entities involved in regional integration schemes; Subscribe to cooperation and technical assistance accords with public and/or private entities whether domestic,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Supranational" title="Supranational">
        supranational
       </a>
       or international. The Committee will be composed of a maximum of 64 acting parliamentary members, 16 per member state, and an equal number of alternates, appointed by the Congress to which they pertain, and with a term of office of at least two years. The meetings shall be conducted by a directors' board consisting of four presidents (one for each member state). The Committee will ordinarily meet twice a year, and extraordinarily whenever summoned by any of its five presidents. Meetings are held in the territory of each member state on a successive and alternating basis. Decision Making: Meetings of the Joint Parliamentary Committee will only be valid when attended by parliamentary delegations from all member states. Decisions by the Joint Parliamentary Committee will be made by consensus vote of the majority of the members accredited by the respective Congresses of each member state. Portuguese and Spanish are the official languages of the Joint Parliamentary Committee.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Trade_Commission">
        Trade Commission
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Trade Commission">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1918" data-file-width="3612" height="117" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg/220px-Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg/330px-Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg/440px-Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sao_Paulo_Stock_Exchange.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Stock_Exchange" title="São Paulo Stock Exchange">
          São Paulo Stock Exchange
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Trade Commission will assist the Mercosur executive body, always striving to apply the instruments of common trade policy agreed to by the member states for operation of the customs unification. The commission should also follow up on the development of issues and matters related to common trade policies, the intra-Mercosur trade and trade with other countries. The Commission will have five actual members and four alternates, with each member nation's indicating a member. The Trade Commission shall exert every effort to apply common trade policy instruments such as: trade agreements with other countries or international entities; administrative/commercial product lists; final adaptation system for Mercosur customs unification; rrigin system;
       <a href="/wiki/Free-trade_zone" title="Free-trade zone">
        free-trade zone
       </a>
       system, special customs areas and export processing zones; system to discourage unfair trade practices; elimination and harmonization of tariff restrictions; nonmember country safeguard systems; customs coordination and harmonization;
       <a href="/wiki/Consumer_protection" title="Consumer protection">
        consumer protection
       </a>
       systems; and export incentive harmonization.
      </p>
      <p>
       Furthermore, the trade commission should speak out regarding the issues raised by the member states regarding application and compliance with common offshore tariffs and other common trade policy instruments. The commission shall meet at least once a month, as well as whenever asked to by the Mercosur executive agency or by a member state. The commission can take decisions entailing administration and application of trade policies adopted under Southern Common Market, and whenever necessary submit proposals to the executive body regarding regulation of the areas under its authority; additionally, it can propose new guidelines or modify those in existence in Mercosur trade and customs matters. In this respect, the trade commission can propose a change in the import duty on specific items under common external tariffs, including cases referring to development of new Mercosur production activities. To better achieve its objectives, the trade commission can create technical committees targeting direction and supervision of the work it engages in. It can also adopt internal operating regulations. Proposals and decisions of the trade commission will be taken by a consensus of the representatives indicated by each member nation. Any disputes ensuing from the application, interpretation or compliance with the acts issued by the trade commission are referred to the Mercosur executive body, and should be resolved using the directives set forth in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dispute_Resolution" title="Dispute Resolution">
        Dispute Resolution
       </a>
       System adopted under Southern Common Market.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="International_jurisdiction_over_contractual_matters">
        International jurisdiction over contractual matters
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: International jurisdiction over contractual matters">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <div style="width:52px">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/>
          </a>
         </div>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          This section
          <b>
           does not
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">
            cite
           </a>
           any
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">
            sources
           </a>
          </b>
          .
          <span class="hide-when-compact">
           Please help
           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">

           </a>

            adding citations to reliable sources

           . Unsourced material may be challenged and
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">

           </a>

           </i>
          </small>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="599" data-file-width="801" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG/220px-Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG/330px-Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG/440px-Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Asunci%C3%B3n_-_Tribunal_del_Mercosur.JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Court of Mercosur, in the city of
         <a href="/wiki/Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Asunción">
          Asunción
         </a>
         , Paraguay
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The rules on litigation jurisdiction over contractual matters will apply to disputes arising from
       <a href="/wiki/Civil_law_(common_law)" title="Civil law (common law)">
        civil
       </a>
       or commercial international contracts between private-law legal entities or individuals provided that: They are domiciled or headquartered in different member states: At least one of the parties to the contract is domiciled or headquartered in any member state and, additionally, has made a choice of jurisdiction in favor of a court in one of the member states. In this case, there must be a reasonable connection between the jurisdiction chosen and the controversy. The scope of the application of the international jurisdiction guidelines over contractual matters excludes the following: legal relationships between bankrupt entities/individuals and their creditors and any other analogous proceedings (especially concordatas composition with creditors); matters under agreements involving family and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Succession_law" title="Succession law">
        succession law
       </a>
       ; social security contracts; administrative contracts; employment contracts; consumer sales contracts; transport contracts; insurance policies; and rights in rem.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Choice_of_jurisdiction">
        Choice of jurisdiction
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Choice of jurisdiction">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Courts in member nations to whose jurisdiction the contracted parties have agreed to submit the matter in writing will have jurisdiction to settle controversies stemming from civil or commercial international contracts.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Agreement_of_choice">
        Agreement of choice
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Agreement of choice">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="2008" height="329" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg/220px-Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg/330px-Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg/440px-Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Aquarius_before_installation_in_its_transport_canister.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The
         <a href="/wiki/SABIA-Mar" title="SABIA-Mar">
          SABIA-Mar
         </a>
         , scheduled to launch in 2017, is a
         <b>
          Brazilian/Argentine
         </b>
         earth observation satellite.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The jurisdiction can be agreed on at the time the contract is signed, during the life of the contract, or even when the dispute actually arises. The validity and effects of the choice of venue will be governed by the law of the member nations that normally have jurisdiction to hear the case, always resorting to the law most favorable to the validity of the contract. Whether or not jurisdiction is chosen, such jurisdiction will be prorogated in favor of the courts of the member state where the proceedings are in fact filed, provided the respondent voluntarily allows this in an affirmative and unfeigned way.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Subsidiary_jurisdiction">
        Subsidiary jurisdiction
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Subsidiary jurisdiction">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Should the contracted parties not agree on courts competent to settle disputes, the member state chosen by the plaintiff of the case has jurisdiction—the court of the place where the contract is to be performed, the court of the domicile of the respondent, or the court of the
       <a href="/wiki/Domicile_(law)" title="Domicile (law)">
        domicile
       </a>
       , or headquarters of the claimant when the latter can show that it has done its part. For purposes of item (i) above the place of performance of the contract is the member state where the obligations on which the claim is based have been or should be performed, taking into consideration the following: For contracts involving certain specific items, the place where they existed at the time of contract signing; For contracts involving specific items according to their type, the place of domicile of the debtor at the time of contract signing; For contracts involving
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fungible" title="Fungible">
        fungible
       </a>
       items, the place of domicile of the debtor at the time of conclusion of the contract; and For service rendering contracts:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        If in regard to items, this the place where they were at the time of contract signing.
       </li>
       <li>
        If effectiveness is related to any special place, this is the place where they were to produce effects.
       </li>
       <li>
        In all other cases, this is the place of domicile of the debtor at the time of contract signing. For purposes of application of second item above for determination of the domicile of the respondent in a contractual dispute involving individuals, the following will be taken into consideration: The habitual residence: On a subsidiary basis, the central place of business; and In the absence of any such considerations, the place where found, meaning the actual residence. When dealing with a legal entity, the determination of the domicile will be based on where the administrative headquarters have been set up. The claim plaintiff can, as an alternative, file in any of the places where the legal entity has branches, establishments, agencies or any other type of representation. Legal entities headquartered in any member state that have concluded contracts with any other member state can be sued in the courts of this latter state should there be any dispute as to the construction and implementation of the obligations regulated by contract. In the event there is a codefendant, a suit on contractual matters can be adjudicated with the courts of jurisdiction in the territory of the domicile of any of the parties to the litigation. Additionally, any claims entailing personal
        <a href="/wiki/Collateral_contract" title="Collateral contract">
         collateral
        </a>
        rights or intervention of nonmember states in contractual obligations can be filed with the court hearing the main proceeding.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Counterclaims">
        Counterclaims
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Counterclaims">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       In the event of there being a counterclaim based on any act or fact that served as the basis for the main proceeding, the courts hearing the main proceeding will be competent to hear any counterclaims that may arise.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Educational_integration">
        Educational integration
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Educational integration">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">

      <div class="thumb tright">

        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_(USP).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1148" data-file-width="1717" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg/220px-Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg/330px-Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg/440px-Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28USP%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Cidade_universit%C3%A1ria_da_Universidade_de_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_(USP).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The
         <a href="/wiki/University_of_S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="University of São Paulo">
          University of São Paulo
         </a>
         , in
         <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">
          São Paulo
         </a>
         , Brazil, is one of the most highly esteemed university institutions in the region of Mercosur.
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
          <a href="#cite_note-35">
           [35]
          </a>
         </sup>
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">
          <a href="#cite_note-36">
           [36]
          </a>
         </sup>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Based on the premise that education is a fundamental factor in the regional
       <a href="/wiki/Regional_integration" title="Regional integration">
        integration
       </a>
       process, educational courses at the primary or junior high level, provided that they do not entail technical studies, will be recognized by member states as being on the same level for all member nations. Likewise, to facilitate continuing education, course certificates issued by an institution accredited in one of the member states is valid in all other member states. Nontechnical primary and junior high level studies that have not been completed are accredited by any member state, thereby allowing course conclusion in another member nation. Studies are completed using an equivalency table to determine the level achieved.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Regional_technical_commission">
        Regional technical commission
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Regional technical commission">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       A regional technical commission harmonizes mechanisms for accreditation across member nations, and resolves any situation not be covered by the equivalency table. This commission includes delegations from the ministries of education of each member nation, and meets whenever at least two member states think it necessary. Meeting sites are established on a rotating basis. Any disputes among member states as a result of application, construction, or noncompliance regarding provisions related to education are initially resolved by direct diplomatic negotiations. Should the countries not reach an accord or only partially resolve the dispute, they resort to procedures set out in the
       <a href="/wiki/Dispute_resolution" title="Dispute resolution">
        dispute resolution
       </a>
       system. Should the member nations enter into a bilateral convention or accord with provisions more favorable to their students, the member states in question can apply whichever provisions they consider most advantageous.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Free_trade_zones">
        Free trade zones
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Free trade zones">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>

      </div>
      <p>
       The member nations can have commercial free-trade zones, industrial free-trade zones, export processing zones, and special customs areas, all of which target providing merchandise marketed or produced in these areas with treatment different from that afforded in their respective customs territories.
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2013)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       Uruguay's Vice-President
       <a href="/wiki/Danilo_Astori" title="Danilo Astori">
        Danilo Astori
       </a>
       said the issue of a free trade agreement with the United States must be dealt and that "opportunities must be built". He also said that "each Mercosur country should have a multiplicity of memberships. Mercosur must have joint international policies, an agreement on moderate protection from third parties and above all must have agreements with other trade blocks".
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">
        <a href="#cite_note-37">
         [37]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tariffs">
        Tariffs
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Tariffs">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The member states can assess merchandise from these areas with the common external tariff used for Mercosur merchandise, or, in the case of certain special products, the domestic tariff prevailing in each individual state. In this way, the products from the free-trade zones can have the more favorable tax treatment established under Southern Common Market, given to the merchandise produced in the normal customs zones of each member state or, in the case of certain special products, can have the normal customs treatment prevailing in each nation. Products coming from outside of Mercosur are highly taxed so that local companies do not feel the need to compete with large international companies.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Safeguards">
        Safeguards
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Safeguards">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       Products produced or marketed in the
       <a href="/wiki/Free-trade_zone" title="Free-trade zone">
        free-trade zones
       </a>
       of each member nation will be eligible for the safeguard system whenever this entails an increase not provided for in imports, but capable of causing damages or threatened damages to the importer country.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Incentives">
        Incentives
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Incentives">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2667" data-file-width="4000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg/220px-Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg/330px-Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg/440px-Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Arena-da-Amazonia-2014.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The city of
         <a href="/wiki/Manaus" title="Manaus">
          Manaus
         </a>
         , Brazil, has a free-trade zone.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       In the event of the producing nation's granting special incentives for production from the free-trade zones that are not compatible with the corresponding guidelines established under the
       <a href="/wiki/General_Agreement_on_Tariffs_and_Trade" title="General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade">
        General Agreement on Tariffs and Trade
       </a>
       (GATT), the member nation can make any adjustments needed to return the situation to equilibrium.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Creation">
        Creation
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Creation">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The member nations agreed that any free-trade zones that in August 1994 were already in operation could operate normally under Mercosur, along with any that are set up in light of legal guidelines prevailing or in course in congress during this same time period. This means that a member nation can no longer create new free-trade zones that are more privileged. Mercosur is an effective agreement for its members.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Manaus_and_Tierra_del_Fuego_FTZs">
        Manaus and Tierra del Fuego FTZs
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Manaus and Tierra del Fuego FTZs">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The actual implementation of Mercosur will not affect the special
       <a href="/wiki/Manaus" title="Manaus">
        Manaus
       </a>
       , Brazil, and
       <a href="/wiki/Tierra_del_Fuego_Province,_Argentina" title="Tierra del Fuego Province, Argentina">
        Tierra del Fuego
       </a>
       , Argentina, free-trade zones organized in light of their special geographic situations. These two free-trade zones may continue normal operations until 2013.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Reciprocal_promotion_and_protection">
        Reciprocal promotion and protection
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Reciprocal promotion and protection">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <div style="width:52px">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/>
          </a>
         </div>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          This section
          <b>
           does not
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">
            cite
           </a>
           any
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">
            sources
           </a>
          </b>
          .
          <span class="hide-when-compact">
           Please help
           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit">
            improve this section
           </a>
           by
           <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">
            adding citations to reliable sources
           </a>
           . Unsourced material may be challenged and
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">
            removed
           </a>
           .
          </span>
          <small>
           <i>
            (July 2017)
           </i>
          </small>
          <small class="hide-when-compact">
           <i>
