            <a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">
             Learn how and when to remove this template message
            </a>
            )
           </i>
          </small>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="538" data-file-width="353" height="335" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg/220px-CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg/330px-CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/a4/CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:CUPULAMERCOSUL.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Celso_Amorim" title="Celso Amorim">
          Celso Amorim
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">
          Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva
         </a>
         ,
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A9rgio_Cabral" title="Sérgio Cabral">
          Sérgio Cabral
         </a>
         during the leadership of Mercosur/Mercosul.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The nations subscribing to the
       <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Treaty of Asunción">
        Asunción Treaty
       </a>
       consider that the creation and maintenance of conditions favorable to individual or corporate investment for the jurisdiction of one of the member states in the territory of another state is essential to intensify the economic cooperation targeted so as to accelerate the integration process among all four member states. In this context, Argentina, Uruguay, Paraguay and Brazil signed on 1 January 1994 in the city of
       <a href="/wiki/Colonia_del_Sacramento" title="Colonia del Sacramento">
        Colonia del Sacramento
       </a>
       , Uruguay, the Colonia Protocol for the Reciprocal Promotion and Protection of Mercosur Investments (Colonia Protocol). It was established in this protocol that investments under Mercosur by investors resident or domiciled in the territory of any member state will be entitled to treatment no less favorable than that accorded by the other member state to national investors or nonmember states.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Investors">
        Investors
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Investors">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       For the purposes of constructing the
       <a href="/wiki/Colonia_(United_States)" title="Colonia (United States)">
        Colonia
       </a>
       Protocol, investors are considered to be: Individuals who are citizens of any of the member nations or that reside there on a permanent basis or are domiciled there, with due regard for legislation prevailing in such territory; Legal entities organized pursuant to the legislation of one of the member nations that are headquartered there; and Legal entities organized in the territory where the investment is made, actually and directly or indirectly controlled by the legal entities or individuals mentioned above.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Investment">
        Investment
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Investment">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The term investment includes all types of assets such as: movable or immovable property, such as rights in rem and guarantee in rem rights; shares, corporate holdings and any other type of corporate participation; credit instruments and rights that may have an economic value; intellectual property rights or materials, Including copyrights and
       <a href="/wiki/Industrial_property" title="Industrial property">
        industrial property
       </a>
       rights such as patents, industrial drawings, trademarks, commercial names, technical procedures, know-how and goodwill; Economic concessions involving
       <a href="/wiki/Public_law" title="Public law">
        public law
       </a>
       , such as research, cultivation, extraction or natural resource exploration concessions.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Freedom_to_invest">
        Freedom to invest
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Freedom to invest">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="2576" height="164" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG/220px-Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG/330px-Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG/440px-Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Frontera_Brasil-Uruguay.JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Brazil–Uruguay international border
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The nation receiving the investment cannot avail itself of unjustified or discriminatory means capable of restricting the investor's freedom to manage, maintain, use, enjoy and dispose of its investments.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tax">
        Tax
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Tax">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The member states are not however obligated to extend to investors in the other nations signatory to the Colonia Protocol the
       <a href="/wiki/Cost%E2%80%93benefit_analysis" title="Cost–benefit analysis">
        benefits
       </a>
       of any treatment, preference or
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Privilege_(legal_ethics)" title="Privilege (legal ethics)">
        privilege
       </a>
       resulting from international accords relating fully or partially to tax matters.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Exceptions">
        Exceptions
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Exceptions">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       In addition, the member nations can temporarily establish a list of exceptions where the new treatment will not yet prevail.
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg/220px-Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg/330px-Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg/440px-Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marco_das_3_fronteiras.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Landmark of the Three Borders – Argentina, Brazil, and Paraguay, in
         <a href="/wiki/Foz_do_Igua%C3%A7u" title="Foz do Iguaçu">
          Foz do Iguaçu
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       In this way, the various member nations decided to except the following economic sectors:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         Argentina:
        </b>
        ownership of real estate on the frontier strip, air transportation, naval industry, nuclear power plants, uranium mining, insurance and fishery;
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Brazil:
        </b>
        mineral prospecting and mining; use of
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hydraulic_energy" title="Hydraulic energy">
         hydraulic energy
        </a>
        ; health care; television and radio broadcasting and telecommunications in general, acquisition or leasing of rural properties; participation in the financial
        <a href="/wiki/Intermediation" title="Intermediation">
         intermediation
        </a>
        , insurance, social security and capitalization systems; chartering and cabotage as well as inland navigation;
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Paraguay:
        </b>
        ownership of real property on the frontier strip; communications, including radio and television broadcasting; air, sea and land transportation; electricity, water and telephone services; prospecting for hydrocarbons and strategic minerals; import and refining of petroleum derivatives and postal services;
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         Uruguay:
        </b>
        electricity; hydrocarbons; basic petrochemicals, atomic energy; prospecting for strategic minerals; financial intermediation; railways, telecommunications; radio broadcasting; press and audiovisual means.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Expropriation_and_compensation">
        Expropriation and compensation
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Expropriation and compensation">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The member nations undertook to do nothing to
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nationalize" title="Nationalize">
        nationalize
       </a>
       or expropriate investments in their territories that pertain to investors from the signatory countries, unless such measures are taken based on public need. In such case, nothing discriminatory can be done, but everything must be implemented by due legal process. Compensation for the investment holder that is expropriated or nationalized should be both adequate and effective, and made in advance, based on the real investment value determined at the time the decision is publicly announced by the proper authorities. This payment will be updated until actual payment, and the affected investor will receive interest.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transfers">
        Transfers
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Transfers">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The original member state investors will be ensured free transfer of their investments and any earnings thereon. These transfers can be made in freely convertible currency, using the
       <a href="/wiki/Exchange_rate" title="Exchange rate">
        exchange rate
       </a>
       prevailing on the market pursuant to the procedures established by the member state receiving the investment. Member nations cannot adopt any exchange measures restricting free transfer of the funds invested or from activities exercised in their respective territories.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Role_and_potential">
        Role and potential
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Role and potential">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:299px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1357" data-file-width="2500" height="161" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg/297px-Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg/446px-Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg/594px-Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg 2x" width="297"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Foto_oficial_49%C2%B0_Cumbre_del_Mercosur.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Plenary Session of the 49th Mercosur Summit in
         <a href="/wiki/Asunci%C3%B3n" title="Asunción">
          Asuncion
         </a>
         , December 28, 2015.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Some South Americans see Mercosur as giving the capability to combine resources to balance the activities of other global economic powers, especially the
       <a href="/wiki/North_American_Free_Trade_Agreement" title="North American Free Trade Agreement">
        North American Free Trade Agreement
       </a>
       (NAFTA) and the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">
        <a href="#cite_note-38">
         [38]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The organization could also potentially pre-empt the
       <a href="/wiki/Free_Trade_Area_of_the_Americas" title="Free Trade Area of the Americas">
        Free Trade Area of the Americas
       </a>
       (FTAA);
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">
        <a href="#cite_note-39">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
       however, over half of the current Mercosur member countries rejected the FTAA proposal at the IV Cumbre de las Américas (
       <a href="/wiki/4th_Summit_of_the_Americas" title="4th Summit of the Americas">
        IV Summit of the Americas
       </a>
       ) in Argentina in 2005.
      </p>
      <p>
       The development of Mercosur was arguably weakened by
       <a href="/wiki/1998%E2%80%932002_Argentine_great_depression" title="1998–2002 Argentine great depression">
        the collapse of the Argentine economy in 2001
       </a>
       and it has still seen internal conflicts over trade policy, between Brazil and Argentina, Argentina and Uruguay, Paraguay and Brazil, etc. In addition, many obstacles must be addressed before the development of a common currency in Mercosur.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">
        <a href="#cite_note-40">
         [40]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In 2004, Mercosur signed a cooperation agreement with the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Andean_Community_of_Nations" title="Andean Community of Nations">
        Andean Community of Nations
       </a>
       trade bloc (CAN) and they published a joint letter of intent for future negotiations towards integrating all of South America.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">
        <a href="#cite_note-41">
         [41]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The prospect of increased political integration within the organization, as per the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       and advocated by some, is still uncertain.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
        <a href="#cite_note-42">
         [42]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Bolivia, also a member of CAN and an associate member of Mercosur before the UNASUR process started, plays a crucial part in relations, says Marion Hörmann, since Bolivia is traditionally seen as a mediator between the Andean countries and the rest of South America.
       <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110927084954/http://www.inwent.org/ez/articles/168821/index.en.shtml" rel="nofollow">
        Regional Integration: Key Role for Bolivia
       </a>
      </p>
      <p>
       The bloc comprises a population of more than
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_population" title="List of countries by population">
        270 million people
       </a>
       , and the combined Gross Domestic Product of the full-member nations is in excess of US$3.0 trillion a year (
       <a href="/wiki/Purchasing_power_parity" title="Purchasing power parity">
        Purchasing power parity
       </a>
       , PPP) according to
       <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">
        International Monetary Fund
       </a>
       (IMF) numbers, making Mercosur the
       <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP)">
        fifth-largest
       </a>
       economy in the World. It is the fourth-largest trading bloc after the European Union.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
        <a href="#cite_note-43">
         [43]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The working of Mercosur has not met with universal approval within interested countries. Chile has to a certain extent preferred to pursue bilateral agreements with trading partners, and there have been calls from Uruguayan politicians to follow this example.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">
        <a href="#cite_note-44">
         [44]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="FTA_with_third_parties">
        FTA with third parties
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: FTA with third parties">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:311px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="420" data-file-width="699" height="186" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg/309px-Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg/464px-Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg/618px-Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg 2x" width="309"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Placas_de_ve%C3%ADculos_do_Mercosul_mercosur.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Mercosur common plates, in use since January 2016
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       With the 2005 cooperation agreement with Mercosur, the
       <a href="/wiki/Andean_Community" title="Andean Community">
        Andean Community
       </a>
       gained four new associate members: Argentina, Brazil, Paraguay, and Uruguay. These four Mercosur members were granted associate membership by the Andean Council of Foreign Ministers meeting in an enlarged session with the Commission (of the Andean Community) on 7 July 2005. This move reciprocates the actions of Mercosur, which granted associate membership to all the Andean Community nations by virtue of the Economic Complementarity Agreements (
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Free_Trade_Agreement" title="Free Trade Agreement">
        Free Trade Agreements
       </a>
       ) signed between the CAN and individual Mercosur members.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">
        <a href="#cite_note-45">
         [45]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Mercosur signed free trade agreements with Israel in December 2007,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">
        <a href="#cite_note-46">
         [46]
        </a>
       </sup>
       with Egypt in August 2010,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">
        <a href="#cite_note-47">
         [47]
        </a>
       </sup>
       the
       <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">
        State of Palestine
       </a>
       in December 2011
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">
        <a href="#cite_note-48">
         [48]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">
        Lebanon
       </a>
       on December 18, 2014.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">
        <a href="#cite_note-49">
         [49]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In 2016, Brazilian presidents,
       <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">
        Dilma Rousseff
       </a>
       and later
       <a href="/wiki/Michel_Temer" title="Michel Temer">
        Michel Temer
       </a>
       , along with Argentine President
       <a href="/wiki/Mauricio_Macri" title="Mauricio Macri">
        Macri
       </a>
       have placed pressure to negotiate a
       <a href="/wiki/Free-trade_area" title="Free-trade area">
        free trade agreement
       </a>
       between Mercosur and the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       and other Latin American nations.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">
        <a href="#cite_note-50">
         [50]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Further_reading">
        Further reading
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Mercosur&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Further reading">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Samuel A. Arieti,
        <i>
         The Role of MERCOSUR as a Vehicle for Latin American Integration,
        </i>
        <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Journal_of_International_Law" title="Chicago Journal of International Law">
         Chicago Journal of International Law
        </a>
        , vol. 6 (2005/2006), pp. 761–773.
       </li>
       <li>
        Rivera, Salvador.
        <b>
         Latin American Unification: A History of Political and Economic Integration Efforts
        </b>
        . North Carolina: McFarland Press, 2014
       </li>
       <li>
        Rivera, Salvador. "Jacob K. Javits and Latin American Economic Integration." Cuaderno de Negocios Internacionales e Integración." 13 no. 64/65 July–December 2007.
       </li>
